Nothing to worry aboutit's just a milestone update from Shopify. You said: Where can i see that subscriber in my shopify dashboard and how can i convert them into sales ChatGPT said: Heres how you can find the subscriber in your Shopify dashboard and turn them into sales:  Where to See Your Email Subscriber in Shopify Your email subscribers are stored as customers in Shopify. Steps to view subscribers: Log in to your Shopify admin:https://admin.shopify.com/ Go to Customers (left-hand menu). At the top, click on Segments. Look for a segment called Email subscribers or Subscribed to email marketing. Youll see your new subscriber listed there with a green Subscribed tag.  How to Turn That Subscriber Into Sales Here are practical ways to monetize your new email subscriber:  1. Send a Welcome Email Use Shopify Email or any email app like Klaviyo. Include: A warm Thank you for subscribing A discount code (e.g., WELCOME10) A link to your best-selling product Why?Welcome emails have some of the highest conversion rates.  2. Set Up an Automated Email Flow Automation helps convert subscribers on autopilot. Examples: Welcome series  Introduce your brand + discount Abandoned cart emails  Invite them back to complete purchase Product recommendations  Show relevant items  3. Offer a Limited-Time Promo Subscribers respond well to urgency. Example: Your 10% discount expires in 24 hours!  4. Highlight Your Best Products Send a curated email featuring: Top sellers Customer favorites New arrivals  5. Provide Value, Not Just Promotions Build trust with content like: Tips related to your niche How-to guides Behind-the-scenes stories This increases engagement  more sales. You said: I want to automate this email whenevers someone subscribes in my store. How do i do automate? ChatGPT said: You can automate your welcome email directly inside Shopify  no coding or third-party apps required. Heres the exact step-by-step setup:  How to Automate a Welcome Email in Shopify Shopify has built-in Marketing Automations that trigger emails when someone subscribes.  STEP 1  Go to Shopify Automations Log into your Shopify Admin. On the left menu, click Marketing. At the top, click Automations. Youll see several templates Shopify provides.  STEP 2  Choose a Welcome Automation Click Create Automation. Select Welcome new subscribers (Shopifys built-in template). This automation triggers whenever someone subscribes to email marketing.  STEP 3  Customize the Email Once the automation loads: Click on the email block inside the workflow. Click Edit email. Replace Shopifys default message with your welcome email content. Add your discount code (e.g., WELCOME10). Edit the subject line and preview text.  STEP 4  Activate the Automation Return to the top-right. Click Turn on Automation. Your welcome email will now automatically send to every new subscriber.   OPTIONAL (BUT POWERFUL)  Add a Delay (e.g., send 2 minutes after subscribing) Click the + button in the workflow  Delay  set 2 minutes.  Add a second follow-up email Example: Email 1 = Welcome Email 2 (2 days later) = Best sellers Email 3 (5 days later) = Social proof or discount reminder  Want me to create a full 3-email automation sequence for you? I can write all emails and tell you exactly how to set them up in Shopify.
